  Variable legend: `pi` is the route, `e_line` the next admissible edge, `B_line` the seal budget.
  Reading: fluid carrier / timed gate / triple essence line.

### Game Theory

- `P1`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P1}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P1}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P1}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P1}}^-)\}\]

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: fluid carrier / timed gate / triple essence line.
  Confidence: strong

- `P2`
  Equation:

  \[y_{\mathrm{P2}}^+ = \operatorname*{argmin}_{y \in \Delta(\mathcal{A})}\{R_{\mathrm{P2}}(y) + \lambda_{\mathrm{P2}} C(y, y_{\mathrm{P2}}^-)\}\]

- `P4`

## Direct Operational Meaning

`f85r1` behaves as `system boot kernel` inside the nine-rosette network.

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f85r1` is a routed network panel rather than a local recipe leaf.

## Mythic Extraction

Across the mythic lenses, `f85r1` is a district in the manuscript's hidden city.

## All-Lens Zero Point

`boot the rosette network and govern volatile traffic by timed gates`

## Dense One-Sentence Compression

`f85r1` = boot the rosette network and govern volatile traffic by timed gates.
